#!/usr/bin/python

import sys

accepted_ans = set()
highest_ans_ids=[]
curr_ans_ids=[]

highest_owner_id = -1
prev_owner_id = -1
owner_id = -1

ans_id = -1

output=""

for line in sys.stdin:          # For ever line in the input from stdin
    line = line.strip()         # Remove trailing characters

    owner_id, ans_id = line.split("\t")
    if int(float(owner_id)) == -1:
        accepted_ans.add(ans_id)
    elif prev_owner_id == -1:
        if ans_id in accepted_ans:
            prev_owner_id = owner_id
            curr_ans_ids.append(ans_id) #Store in array
    elif prev_owner_id == owner_id:
        if ans_id in accepted_ans:
            curr_ans_ids.append(ans_id) #Store in array
    else:
        if highest_owner_id <> -1:  #check previous highest count, and if lower, replace with current
            if len(highest_ans_ids) < len(curr_ans_ids):
                highest_ans_ids = curr_ans_ids
                highest_owner_id = prev_owner_id
        if highest_owner_id == -1:
                highest_ans_ids = curr_ans_ids
                highest_owner_id = prev_owner_id

        prev_owner_id = owner_id
        curr_ans_ids=[]
        if ans_id in accepted_ans:
            curr_ans_ids.append(ans_id)

if prev_owner_id == owner_id:  # Don't forget the last key/value pair
        if highest_owner_id <> -1:  #check previous highest count, and if lower, replace with current
            if len(highest_ans_ids) < len(curr_ans_ids):
                highest_ans_ids = curr_ans_ids
                highest_owner_id = prev_owner_id
            if highest_owner_id == -1:
                highest_ans_ids = curr_ans_ids
                highest_owner_id = prev_owner_id

for ans_id in highest_ans_ids:
    if len(output) == 0:
        output = ans_id
    elif len(output) > 0:
        output = output + ", " + ans_id
print("{0} -> {1}, {2}".format(highest_owner_id,len(highest_ans_ids), output))
